d oc u me nts ma y i n cl u de h os pital rec or ds, cli nical a n d office c harts, la b orat or y

s o urce d oc u m e nts. 
A s u bjec t e nr oll me nt l o g is t o be c o m plete d at eac h st u d y site.  Data rec or de d o n t he 
e nr oll me nt l o g are t o i ncl u de a s u bject i de ntifier, t he date of e nr oll me nt, a n d t he reas o n 
t he s u bject was n ot e ntere d (if a p plica ble).  All s u bjects i nitiall y c o nsi dere d f or 
e nr oll me nt are t o b e rec or de d i n t his l o g.

re vie w, a n d re g ulat or y i ns pecti o n(s), pr o vi di n g dir ect access t o s o urce data d oc u me nts.

t he s u bject's ri g hts, s afet y, or well- bei n g a n d/ or t h e c o m plete ness, acc urac y a n d relia bilit y 
of t he st u d y d ata. T his i ncl u des e x a m ples s uc h as i na p pr o priate c o nse nt, err ors i n dr u g 
d osi n g , or la c k of re p orti n g of s afet y d ata.
